<div class="wprm-recipe wprm-recipe-snippet wprm-recipe-template-cil-lemon-limes-snippet"><a href="#recipe" data-recipe="11503" style="color: #4a4a4a;background-color: #ffffff;border-color: #9b9b9b;border-radius: 1px;padding: 5px 8px;" class="wprm-recipe-jump wprm-recipe-link wprm-jump-to-recipe-shortcode wprm-block-text-normal wprm-recipe-jump-inline-button wprm-recipe-link-inline-button wprm-color-accent">Jump to Recipe</a>
</div><h2><strong>Apple Pie Filling Recipe</strong></h2>
<p>Today, I&#8217;m sharing a mouth-watering apple pie filling recipe that&#8217;s not only delicious for an instant dessert fix but also perfect for preserving those autumn flavors.</p>
<p>You&#8217;ll need crisp, tart apples like Granny Smiths, a sprinkle of cinnamon, a touch of nutmeg, a hint of lemon zest, and a touch of sweetness to tie it all together. Simmer it to perfection, and you&#8217;ve got a versatile filling ready to grace pies, tarts, and even turnovers.</p>
<p>Plus, this recipe is a champ for canning or freezing, ensuring you can enjoy that warm apple goodness year-round.</p>
<p>So, whether you&#8217;re diving in right away or stocking up for later, this recipe&#8217;s the perfect choice!</p>
<h2><strong>Apple Pie Filling for Canning</strong></h2>
<p>This is the perfect pie apple pie filling recipe for canning or freezing. Use a <a href="https://www.walmart.com/search?q=quart+jar+for+canning" data-wpel-link="external" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">quart jar for canning</a> or a <a href="https://goto.walmart.com/c/1354032/565706/9383?veh=aff&amp;sourceid=imp_000011112222333344&amp;u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.walmart.com%2Fsearch%3Fq%3Dgallon-sized%2Bfreezer%2Bbag" data-wpel-link="external" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">gallon-sized freezer bag</a> for freezing. You&#8217;ll put the same amount in either container. The freezer bag can be laid and pressed flat for easier and more efficient storage.</p>
<p>I hope you give it a try and let me know what you think in the comments below!</p>
